The Iron Logic of History

Look at this portrait. This is the First Emperor of Qin, or at least how we usually see him. What did he truly look like? No one knows. This is merely a Ming Dynasty artist’s imagination. But in our middle school textbooks, we’ve all memorized this single line: 'In the 26th year of King Zheng (221 BC), Qin annexed the six states and established an unprecedented Great Unity.'

So, when we speak of Qin Shi Huang, we say he "unified China," right? We look at the map and see a seamless empire. But pay attention—I’ve marked a tiny red dot here. Southwest of Puyang County, Henan. What is it? It’s a state called Wei. And Qin Shi Huang failed to unify it. Wei was a small fiefdom of the Zhou royalty; its lineage survived 37 generations, and the First Emperor never managed to wipe it out. It wasn’t until his son, the Second Emperor, took over that Wei was finally extinguished.

Let me ask you: if the Great Qin failed to conquer this 0.3% of territory in 221 BC, does history record it that way? Do our annals say: 'In 221 BC, Qin unified China—excluding the State of Wei'? No. Why? Because Wei was a non-issue. You can run, but you cannot hide; your annexation was only a matter of time. You’re just 0.3%—so what if you’re not unified yet? You’re already in the bag.

Now look at this couplet written by Sun Yat-sen: 'A hall of flowers intoxicates three thousand guests; a single sword’s frost chills forty prefectures.' Yu Youren wrote it, too. Why "forty prefectures"? Pure bluster! There were only fourteen at the time. Who started this bragging? It was during the Five Dynasties and Ten Kingdoms period. Amidst the chaos, there was a crucial state called Wuyue (Hangzhou).

Please note: Wuyue declared independence at the end of the Tang Dynasty. It remained independent through the 53 years of the Five Dynasties. Even when the Song Dynasty was founded, Wuyue stood alone. Think about it: Wuyue stood independent for 77 years. But in the end? You couldn't escape. Unified!

Yet, history doesn't record: 'In 960 AD, the Song Emperor unified China (brackets: excluding Wuyue).' No! When the grandson finally tried to appease the Song Emperor with a mountain of jewels, the Emperor laughed: 'These are already items in my own storehouse; why bother "offering" them to me?' He meant: Your land is already my land.

Taiwan has only been apart for 51 years. Not even 77 yet. Do you think you can escape? You cannot.

That is the crux of the matter. History doesn't record 'Qin unified China except Wei,' nor 'Song unified China except Wuyue.' Consequently, it will not record: 'In 1949, the People’s Republic unified China, except Taiwan.' History doesn't write like that.

I am telling you: Taiwan is a 'remnant regime' (Pian’an). In the grand annals of history, Taiwan will be nothing more than a single line: 'On such-and-such a day, in such-and-such a year, it was finally unified by China.' That is the cold, hard historical fact.

The Martyrdom of a Rightist

Gansu Province. Jiabiangou Re-education Through Labor Camp.
December 12, 1968. Temperature: -28°C.

The wind in the Gobi Desert does not blow; it flays. It strips the flesh from the bone just as the Party strips the dignity from the man. My name is no longer Li Ao. I am Number 9527. A poetic number, I think, for the greatest Chinese intellect of the last five hundred years to be reduced to a sequence of digits by a regime that cannot count past "one"—one Leader, one Thought, one Voice.

I shovel the frozen excrement from the latrine pits. This is my "rehabilitation." The Camp Commandant, a illiterate peasant who thinks Marx is a brand of sorghum wine, told me that labor would cleanse my bourgeois soul. I told him that if labor was so noble, the donkey would be the Emperor of China. That remark cost me three teeth and two weeks in the "reflection cell," a hole in the ground too small to stand in and too wet to sit in.

They say the Chairman is the "Red Sun in our hearts." A fitting metaphor. He is indeed a sun—a nuclear ball of gas that scorches the earth, dries up the rivers, and blinds anyone foolish enough to look directly at him. Under this Red Sun, we do not grow; we wither.

My crime? "Maliciously attacking the Great Leap Forward." All I did was use a bit of arithmetic. I pointed out that melting down peasant cooking pots to make steel results in two things: useless lumps of metal and peasants who cannot cook. I wrote an essay titled "On the Logical Fallacies of Planting Crops Too Close Together." I cited agricultural texts from the Han Dynasty to the Qing. I argued that physics does not care about revolutionary zeal.

For this, they labeled me an "Ultra-Rightist." A "Running Dog of the Chiang Clique."

Ah, Chiang Kai-shek. The Generalissimo. The Gimo.

In this frozen hell, he has become my God. I close my eyes and I see him. Not the bald, defeated warlord described in the People's Daily, but a shining knight of Confucian virtue. I imagine the island of Taiwan. It must be a paradise. A Greco-Roman utopia of logic, law, and liberty.

I imagine the streets of Taipei. Surely, they are paved with marble. Intellectuals there must walk with their heads held high, wearing silk gowns, discussing philosophy in tea houses without fear of being reported by their own children. In Taiwan, the press must be free—wildly free! I bet a man like me could publish anything there. I bet I could write a book called "The Joy of Criticizing the Government," and Generalissimo Chiang would invite me to tea to thank me for my constructive feedback.

The Interrogation.

I am dragged into the interrogation room. A single lightbulb swings overhead. The Commissar sits behind a desk, smoking a cigarette. The smoke smells like heaven.

"Li Ao," the Commissar says, tossing a file on the table. "You are stubborn. Your fellow prisoners have all confessed. They admit they were poisoned by feudal thoughts. Why can't you just say you love the Party?"

I adjust my broken glasses. One lens is missing, the other is cracked like a spiderweb. "Commissar, I cannot love a Party that treats syntax like a counter-revolutionary crime. I read your wall posters. The grammar is atrocious. You simplified the characters so much that 'love' (愛) no longer has a 'heart' (心) in it. How can I love without a heart?"

The Commissar slams his fist. "You arrogant intellectual stinking ninth! You think you are better than the workers and peasants?"

"I am better," I reply calmly. "Not because of my birth, but because I read books instead of burning them. You talk about the 'New China.' I see only the old tyranny wrapped in new red cloth. Qin Shi Huang buried 460 scholars alive; you have buried 460,000, and you didn't even have the decency to dig the holes first."

"You worship Chiang Kai-shek!" he screams. "You are a spy for the KMT!"

"I am not a spy. I am a patriot," I sneer. "The Republic of China is the legitimate government. The Constitution of 1947 is the only law I recognize. You are the rebels. You are the bandits. You are a temporary stain on 5,000 years of history. Do you think this madness will last? Do you think destroying the Four Olds will erase the memory of the people? One day, this era will be looked upon as a dark comedy, and I... I will be the punchline that stuck in your throat."

The Commissar pulls out his pistol and pistol-whips me across the face. I taste blood. It tastes metallic, like the useless steel from the backyard furnaces.

The Execution Ground.

They drag me out at dawn. They say it is for "Counter-Revolutionary Incitement" and "Refusing to Reform." They tie my hands behind my back with rough hemp rope. They force me to kneel in the snow, alongside a former landlord and a teacher who taught English.

A crowd has gathered. Peasants, students, Red Guards with their armbands. They shout slogans. "Down with Li Ao!" "Crush the reactionary insect!"

I look at them. I do not feel fear. I feel pity. Look at them, foaming at the mouth, waving their little red books. They are not humans; they are a herd. They have traded their brains for a bowl of rice and a sense of belonging.

I refuse to kneel. The guard kicks the back of my knees, but I struggle back up. I will die standing. I will die like a man.

I look to the Southeast. Towards the sea. Towards the island.

Oh, Taiwan. My beautiful, imaginary Taiwan.

I see it so clearly now. The white sun in the blue sky. I see the Generalissimo standing on a balcony, waving to a free and prosperous people. I see myself there, clad not in these rags, but in a sharp suit, holding a pen that is sharper than any sword. In that world, I am a hero. In that world, I am free.

The executioner chambers a round. The metallic clack-clack is the loudest sound in the world.

I take a deep breath. The air is cold, but my blood is boiling with defiance. I will not give them the satisfaction of silence. I will give them a final lesson in history.

"Fools!" I roar, my voice cracking but carrying across the frozen field. "You can kill my body, but you cannot kill the Spirit of the Republic! You are building a castle on sand! History will judge you! The ink of the scholar lasts longer than the blood of the martyr!"

"Ready!" the officer shouts.

I lift my head. I look past the gray sky, past the red flags, staring directly into the eyes of history.

"LONG LIVE THE REPUBLIC OF CHINA!"

"LONG LIVE GENERALISSIMO CHIANG!"

"THE THREE PRINCIPLES OF THE PEOPLE WILL UNIFY CHINA!"

BANG.

(The family of the criminal Li Ao is hereby ordered to pay 0.5 RMB for the cost of the bullet.)

                break;             }         }     } }); // 2. 启动观察者 resultButtonObserver.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true }); //注释代码 CODE2 function getTooltips(str) { let matches = []; tooltipList.forEach((tooltip, index) => { // Adjust the regex to match searchString potentially surrounded by “ and followed by optional punctuation let regex = new RegExp(`(?<=\\b|\\s|^|“)${tooltip.searchString}(?=[.,;!?]?\\b|\\s|”|$)`, 'g'); let match; while ((match = regex.exec(str)) !== null) { matches.push({ start: match.index + (match[0].startsWith('“') ? 1 : 0), // Adjust for potential starting “ end: match.index + match[0].length - (match[0].endsWith('”') ? 1 : 0) - (match[2] ? 1 : 0), tooltipIndex: index }); } }); // Sort by starting position; if two start at the same position, longer match comes first matches.sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start || b.end - b.start - (a.end - a.start)); // Filter out overlaps for (let i = 0; i < matches.length - 1; ) { if (matches[i + 1].start < matches[i].end) { matches.splice(i + 1, 1); // Remove the next match since it overlaps } else { i++; // Move to next match } } return matches; } function applyTooltips(str) { const matches = getTooltips(str); let result = ''; let lastIndex = 0; // 获取当前候选人 ID const currentCandidatePK = campaignTrail_temp.candidate_id; matches.forEach(match => { const tooltip = tooltipList[match.tooltipIndex]; result += str.slice(lastIndex, match.start); // --- 核心逻辑：根据 PK 选取定制文本 --- let finalExplanationText = tooltip.explanationText; try { const customData = JSON.parse(tooltip.explanationText); if (currentCandidatePK && customData[currentCandidatePK]) { finalExplanationText = customData[currentCandidatePK]; } else if (customData.default) { finalExplanationText = customData.default; } } catch (e) { // 如果解析失败，说明它是非定制的普通字符串，保持不变 finalExplanationText = tooltip.explanationText; } // ------------------------------------ result += `${tooltip.searchString}${finalExplanationText}`; lastIndex = match.end; }); result += str.slice(lastIndex); // Add the remainder of the original string return result; } function applyTooltipsToObject(obj) { for (let key in obj) { if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') { obj[key] = applyTooltips(obj[key]); } else if (typeof obj[key] === 'object' && obj[key] !== null) { applyTooltipsToObject(obj[key]); // Recursive call } } } // 只有当玩家在 Code 1 选择了开启（默认）时，才运行注释替换 if (campaignTrail_temp.tooltip_enabled) { applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.questions_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answers_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answer_feedback_json); } /* Welcome to Astro's Variable Headquarters This is a fairly simple function you can add to your mods. It will create a little menu in which the player can view the numbers laid out within the functions. This is a great way to give the player a little more information about your mod. You can duplicate the 'let a = document.createElement('p');' section to add more lines of text. Functions are referenced in text like so: ' + function + '. This will display the number from the function in the text. Global Constants and Variables Definition // ================================================================= // Windows 98 Core CSS Colors const WIN98_GREY = '#C0C0C0'; const WIN98_DARK = '#808080'; const WIN98_BLUE = '#000080'; const WIN98_LIGHT = '#FFFFFF'; const WIN98_BORDER_SIZE = '2px'; // Candidate Primary Keys (PKs) for 2000 ROC Presidential Election const CHEN_PK = 67; // Chen Shui-bian (Deep Green) const LIEN_PK = 68; // Lien Chan (Blue) const SOONG_PK = 69; // James Soong (Orange - Independent/PFP later) const HSU_PK = 1921; // Hsu Hsin-liang (Light Green) const LIAO_PK = 1942; // Li Ao (Yellow) // Data Storage Variables var CurrentPollResults = [];      // Stores the corrected/fogged poll data (Read-Only for Mod UI) var SidebarHideStyleTag = null;   // Stores the

`; const tbody = container.querySelector('#poll_results_tbody'); let totalVote = 0; CurrentPollResults.forEach(data => { totalVote += data.vote; // Find the full candidate data (from CANDIDATE_DATA) // We use the PK to find the corresponding name in CANDIDATE_DATA const fullData = CANDIDATE_DATA.find(c => { // Clean the name from the poll results (e.g., "Chen Shui Bian (DPP)" -> "Chen Shui Bian") const cleanPollName = data.name.replace(/\s*\([^)]*\)/, '').trim(); return c.name === cleanPollName; }) || { name: data.name, partyIconUrl: '', position: 'N/A', description: 'N/A', imageUrl: '' }; // The display name will be the name without the party abbreviation const displayName = fullData.name; // Create the hoverable name element structure const nameContent = ` ${fullData.partyIconUrl ? `` : ''} ${displayName} `; const row = document.createElement('tr'); row.innerHTML = ` ${data.rank} ${nameContent} ${data.vote.toFixed(1)}%

tooltip.style.left = `${leftPos + window.scrollX}px`; // Styling tooltip.style.backgroundColor = '#f8f9fa'; tooltip.style.color = '#212529';           tooltip.style.padding = '15px 20px'; tooltip.style.border = '1px solid #dee2e6'; tooltip.style.borderRadius = '8px'; tooltip.style.boxShadow = '0 6px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)'; tooltip.style.zIndex = '2000'; tooltip.style.whiteSpace = 'normal'; tooltip.style.maxWidth = '300px'; tooltip.style.minWidth = '250px'; document.body.appendChild(tooltip); }); // Mouseout event: Remove Tooltip element.addEventListener('mouseout', function() { const tooltip = document.getElementById(uniqueId); if (tooltip) { tooltip.remove(); } }); }); } /** * Helper function to calculate the 9 voter flow percentages based on the election state. * 使用更通用的字符串匹配来应对 getCrossoverPrediction() 中可能的变化。 */ function getFlowRules(predictionTitle) { // 默认值：三强鼎立 (Gridlock) - 98% 坚守, 1% 跑票给另外两人 let flow = { KMT_to_KMT: 98, KMT_to_DPP: 1, KMT_to_IND: 1, // KMT row DPP_to_KMT: 1, DPP_to_DPP: 98, DPP_to_IND: 1, // DPP row IND_to_KMT: 1, IND_to_DPP: 1, IND_to_IND: 98 // IND row }; // ---------------------------------------------------- // 扁连对决 (Chen-Lien Showdown) - 宋楚瑜 (IND) 票源流向 // ---------------------------------------------------- if (predictionTitle.includes("Chen-Lien")) { // 宋楚瑜票源大流向：70% 坚守, 25% Lien, 5% Chen flow.IND_to_KMT = 25; flow.IND_to_DPP = 5; flow.IND_to_IND = 70; } // ---------------------------------------------------- // 扁宋对决 (Chen-Soong Faceoff) - 连战 (KMT) 票源流向 // ---------------------------------------------------- else if (predictionTitle.includes("Chen-Soong")) { // <-- 修正：使用更通用的 "Chen-Soong" // 连战票源大流向：70% 坚守, 25% Soong, 5% Chen flow.KMT_to_KMT = 70; flow.KMT_to_DPP = 5; flow.KMT_to_IND = 25; } // ---------------------------------------------------- // 连宋对决 (Lien-Soong Clash) - 陈水扁 (DPP) 票源流向 // ---------------------------------------------------- else if (predictionTitle.includes("Lien-Soong")) { // 陈水扁票源大流向：80% 坚守, 15% Lien, 5% Soong flow.DPP_to_KMT = 15; flow.DPP_to_DPP = 80; flow.DPP_to_IND = 5; } // 如果是 Gridlock (三强鼎立) 或 Clear Leader (明确领先)，则返回默认的 98% 坚守。 return flow; } /** * 2. createCrossoverContent() - Crossover Analysis Interface */ /** * 2. createCrossoverContent() - Crossover Analysis Interface */ function createCrossoverContent(container) { // 1. 获取选情预测和动态流动数据 const prediction = getCrossoverPrediction(); const flow = getFlowRules(prediction.title); // 调用新的流动规则函数 // 2. 将数据转换为带百分号的字符串 // KMT (Lien Chan) Row const KMT_HOLD = flow.KMT_to_KMT.toFixed(0) + '%'; const KMT_TO_CHEN = flow.KMT_to_DPP.toFixed(0) + '%'; const KMT_TO_SOONG = flow.KMT_to_IND.toFixed(0) + '%'; // DPP (Chen Shui Bian) Row const DPP_TO_LIEN = flow.DPP_to_KMT.toFixed(0) + '%'; const DPP_HOLD = flow.DPP_to_DPP.toFixed(0) + '%'; const DPP_TO_SOONG = flow.DPP_to_IND.toFixed(0) + '%'; // IND (James Soong) Row const IND_TO_LIEN = flow.IND_to_KMT.toFixed(0) + '%'; const IND_TO_CHEN = flow.IND_to_DPP.toFixed(0) + '%'; const IND_HOLD = flow.IND_to_IND.toFixed(0) + '%'; container.style.textAlign = 'left'; container.innerHTML = `

Crossover Flow Analysis Tool

Current Election State Analysis

${prediction.title}

${prediction.message}

Voter Flow Percentage (%)
Flow OUT (FROM) ↓
Flow IN (TO) →		 Lien Chan (KMT) Chen Shui Bian (DPP) James Soong (IND)
Lien Chan (KMT) Base Hold (${KMT_HOLD}) Lost to Chen (${KMT_TO_CHEN}) Lost to Soong (${KMT_TO_SOONG})
Chen Shui Bian (DPP) Flow to Lien (${DPP_TO_LIEN}) Base Hold (${DPP_HOLD}) Flow to Soong (${DPP_TO_SOONG})
James Soong (IND) Flow to Lien (${IND_TO_LIEN}) Flow to Chen (${IND_TO_CHEN}) Base Hold (${IND_HOLD})
`; } function createVariablesContent(container, e) { const context = e || {}; // 🌟 確保這三行存在，它們為 HTML 模板中的 ${} 提供了值 const attackCount = context.LeeTengHuiAttacks || 0; const Centralway = context.Centralway || 0; const PoliticalReformPromise = context.PoliticalReformPromise || 0; // (以下是正常的 HTML 輸出邏輯) container.style.textAlign = 'left'; container.innerHTML = `

📈 Core Variable Status Tracking (HQ)

Campaign Environment Key Factors

C:\\> run_analysis.exe /v

`; } function createLiPolicyFramework(container, e) { container.style.textAlign = 'left'; // Constant for Li Ao's PK const LI_PK = 1942; // Define policy issues - Tailored for Li Ao (New Party / Intellectual Firebrand) const POLICY_ISSUES = { 32: { name: "Party Coalition", desc: "New Party / Protest Vote" }, 33: { name: "Provincialism", desc: "Mainland Intelligentsia / Chinese Culture" }, 34: { name: "Political Reform", desc: "Deep Blue Iron Vote / Exposing 'Black Gold'" }, 35: { name: "National Identity", desc: "Immediate Unification / One Country Two Systems" }, 36: { name: "Attitude towards Lee Teng-hui", desc: "Vehement Opposition / 'Traitor to the Nation'" } }; // Get Li Ao's policy scores function getLiPolicyScores() { // Default scores based on the provided JSON values const defaultScores = { 32: 1.00, // Party Coalition: Deep Blue (极统派/新党) 33: 0.95, // Provincial: Mostly Mainlanders (强外省文化代表) 34: 0.95, // Political Reform: Blue Iron Vote (蓝营铁票) 35: 0.90, // National identity: Love live ROC! (极统派立场) 36: 0.80 // Attitude towards LTH: Intense Hatred }; if (typeof campaignTrail_temp === 'undefined' || !campaignTrail_temp.candidate_issue_score_json) { console.warn('Policy data not available, returning default Li Ao scores.'); return defaultScores; } const rawData = campaignTrail_temp.candidate_issue_score_json; const scores = {}; let foundCandidate = false; for (const item of rawData) { if (item.fields && item.fields.candidate === LI_PK) { const issueId = item.fields.issue; scores[issueId] = item.fields.issue_score; foundCandidate = true; } } // If we didn't find specific data for Li in the live JSON, use defaults // Otherwise, ensure all keys exist if (!foundCandidate) { return defaultScores; } [32, 33, 34, 35, 36].forEach(issueId => { if (scores[issueId] === undefined) { scores[issueId] = defaultScores[issueId] || 0.0; } }); return scores; } const policyScores = getLiPolicyScores(); // Generate table rows let tableRows = ''; [32, 33, 34, 35, 36].forEach(issueId => { const score = policyScores[issueId]; const issue = POLICY_ISSUES[issueId]; // Determine color and position description based on score let positionDesc = ''; let scoreColor = '#000000'; if (score > 0.5) { positionDesc = 'Deep Blue/Unification Stance'; scoreColor = '#0000FF'; } else if (score > 0) { positionDesc = 'Light Blue/Centrist Stance'; scoreColor = '#4169E1'; } else if (score === 0) { positionDesc = 'Neutral Stance'; scoreColor = '#808080'; } else if (score > -0.5) { positionDesc = 'Light Green/Localist Stance'; scoreColor = '#32CD32'; } else { positionDesc = 'Deep Green/Independence Stance'; scoreColor = '#228B22'; } tableRows += ` ${issue.name} ${score.toFixed(2)} ${issue.desc} ${positionDesc} `; }); container.innerHTML = `

📋 Li Ao Policy Framework

Policy Stance Scores ${tableRows}
Policy Issue Score Description Position Category
Score Explanation

Score Range: -1.0 to +1.0

  • Above +0.5: Deep Blue/Unification Stance
  • 0 to +0.5: Light Blue/Centrist Stance
  • 0: Neutral Stance
  • -0.5 to 0: Light Green/Localist Stance
  • Below -0.5: Deep Green/Independence Stance

C:\\> policy_framework.exe /candidate=Li_Ao

`; } /** * 4. createTrendContent() - Poll Trend Chart Interface */ /** * createTrendContent(container) * Creates the content for the Poll Trend tab, including a dedicated horizontal scrolling wrapper. * FIX: Set fixed height (500px) to force Chart.js to render Y-axis correctly. */ function createTrendContent(container) { const historicalData = compileHistoricalPollData(); // --- 1. 创建水平滚动隔离容器 --- const chartWrapper = document.createElement('div'); chartWrapper.id = 'poll_trend_wrapper'; chartWrapper.style.width = '100%'; chartWrapper.style.height = '100%'; // 启用手动水平滚动 chartWrapper.style.overflowX = 'scroll'; chartWrapper.style.overflowY = 'hidden'; // --- 2. 创建图表容器 --- const chartContainer = document.createElement('div'); chartContainer.id = 'poll_trend_chart_container'; chartContainer.style.width = '100%'; // *** 关键：固定高度 500px，解决 Y 轴渲染问题 *** chartContainer.style.height = '500px'; chartWrapper.appendChild(chartContainer); container.appendChild(chartWrapper); // --- 3. 渲染图表 --- renderPollTrendChart(historicalData); } // ================================================================= // IV. Interface Control Functions (CSS Hide Mode) // ================================================================= /** * addDataCenterButton() * Configures the Mod entry point (both original custom button and hijacked PV button) * and sets up hover effects. */ /** * addDataCenterButton() * Configures the Mod entry point and triggers AUTO-RECORDING of poll data. */ function addDataCenterButton() { // 1. 尝试找到参照物按钮 (View Electoral Map) const refButton = document.getElementById('view_electoral_map'); tabButton.style.borderLeft = '1px solid #FFFFFF'; tabButton.style.borderRight = '1px solid #808080'; tabButton.style.borderBottom = '1px solid #808080'; tabButton.style.backgroundColor = WIN98_GREY; } } }); } // ------------------------------------------------------------------ // Create tab buttons tabs.forEach(tab => { let btn = document.createElement('button'); btn.id = 'tab_' + tab.id; btn.innerText = tab.label; btn.style.fontFamily = 'Tahoma, Geneva, sans-serif'; btn.style.fontSize = '12px'; btn.style.color = '#000000'; btn.style.border = '1px solid #808080'; btn.style.cursor = 'pointer'; btn.style.marginRight = '2px'; } // ================================================================= // V. Initialization Logic (Mutation Observer) // ================================================================= let observerRunning = false; function handleMutations(mutationsList, observer) { if (observerRunning) return; observerRunning = true; // === 【新增】在每个回合加载时自动生成和缓存数据 === // 这样做能够确保 PollAdjustmentCache 始终是最新且完整的 if (typeof generateModData === 'function') { // 注意：我们必须确保 generateModData 能够访问到 e.question_number generateModData(); } // ========================================================== // 这一行是关键，它在每次 Mutation (界面变动，包括加载新问题) 后尝试执行 // 应该调用 addDataCenterButtons 和 hideRawPVData if (typeof addDataCenterButtons === 'function') { addDataCenterButtons(); } if (typeof hideRawPVData === 'function') { hideRawPVData(); } // 并且要确保候选人 hover 效果也生效 if (typeof addCandidateHoverEffects === 'function') { addCandidateHoverEffects(); } // Re-observe if the DOM changes again observer.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true }); observerRunning = false; } // MOD Execution Entry Point let element = document.getElementById('controlElement'); if (!element) { // Only observe once until the control element is added (to prevent infinite loops) let singleObserver = new MutationObserver(handleMutations); singleObserver.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true }); // Add a control element to indicate the mod has started observation let controlElement = document.createElement('div'); controlElement.style.display = 'none'; controlElement.id = 'controlElement'; document.body.appendChild(controlElement); } //关键的恢复原始投票函数 function showOverallResult() { const targetElement = document.getElementById('overall_result'); if (targetElement) { // 这行代码是关键！它会覆盖您的 style_overwrite.innerHTML 中的 !important targetElement.style.setProperty('display', 'block', 'important'); // 如果 ul 子元素也被隐藏，同时显示它 const ulElement = targetElement.querySelector('ul'); if (ulElement) { ulElement.style.setProperty('display', 'block', 'important'); } } } // ================================================================= // VI. Final Election Result Chart Integration // ================================================================= /** * 1. Calculate Actual Election Results & Format for Chart * 获取最终选举结果，并将其格式化为图表所需的格式，作为"下一回合"的数据。 */ /** * 1. Calculate Actual Election Results & Format for Chart * 获取最终选举结果 (修正版：指定读取主候选人，排除副总统) */ function getFinalResultsAsTrendData(nextTurnIndex) { if (!campaignTrail_temp || !campaignTrail_temp.candidate_json) return []; // 安全获取数据的辅助函数 (防止游戏数据未加载导致报错) const getPvp = (index) => { if (campaignTrail_temp.candidate_json[index]) { return campaignTrail_temp.candidate_json[index].pvp; } return 0; }; // 1. 根据您提供的索引获取 PVP (0.35 -> 35.0) // 索引顺序：0=Chen, 2=Soong, 4=Lien, 6=Hsu, 8=Li Ao let final_chen_pvp = getPvp(0) * 100; let final_soong_pvp = getPvp(2) * 100; let final_lien_pvp = getPvp(4) * 100; let final_hsu_pvp = getPvp(6) * 100; let final_liao_pvp = getPvp(8) * 100; let finalData = []; // 2. 手动构建数据对象 (只构建这5个人，绝不会出现副总统) // Chen Shui-bian (Deep Green) if (final_chen_pvp > 0) { finalData.push({ turn: nextTurnIndex, pk: CHEN_PK, // 67 name: "Chen Shui Bian (Actual)", vote: final_chen_pvp, color: "#008000" }); } // Lien Chan (Blue) if (final_lien_pvp > 0) { finalData.push({ turn: nextTurnIndex, pk: LIEN_PK, // 68 name: "Lien Chan (Actual)", vote: final_lien_pvp, color: "#0000FF" }); } // James Soong (Orange) if (final_soong_pvp > 0) { finalData.push({ turn: nextTurnIndex, pk: SOONG_PK, // 69 name: "James Soong (Actual)", vote: final_soong_pvp, color: "#FF8C00" }); } // Hsu Hsin-liang if (final_hsu_pvp > 0) { finalData.push({ turn: nextTurnIndex, pk: HSU_PK, // 1921 name: "Hsu Hsin-liang (Actual)", vote: final_hsu_pvp, color: "#90EE90" }); } // Li Ao if (final_liao_pvp > 0) { finalData.push({ turn: nextTurnIndex, pk: LIAO_PK, // 1942 name: "Li Ao (Actual)", vote: final_liao_pvp, color: "#FFFF00" }); } return finalData; } /** * 2. Open Final Chart Window * 打开最终图表窗口（复用 Win98 风格，但针对最终画面微调） */ /** * openFinalChartWindow() * 打开最终图表窗口 * 结局时调用：isFinalMode = true */ function openFinalChartWindow() { // 1. 准备数据 let historicalData = compileHistoricalPollData(); let maxTurn = 0; if (historicalData.length > 0) { maxTurn = Math.max(...historicalData.map(d => d.turn)); } // 获取真实结果，设为下一回合 const finalResults = getFinalResultsAsTrendData(maxTurn + 1); const combinedData = [...historicalData, ...finalResults]; // 2. 创建窗口 (简略版，只列出核心逻辑) const existingWin = document.getElementById('final_chart_window'); if (existingWin) existingWin.remove(); let mainDiv = document.createElement('div'); mainDiv.id = 'final_chart_window'; mainDiv.style.position = 'fixed'; mainDiv.style.top = '10%'; mainDiv.style.left = '10%'; mainDiv.style.width = '80%'; mainDiv.style.height = '70%'; mainDiv.style.zIndex = '9999'; mainDiv.style.backgroundColor = '#C0C0C0'; mainDiv.style.border = '2px solid #FFFFFF'; mainDiv.style.borderRight = '2px solid #808080'; mainDiv.style.borderBottom = '2px solid #808080'; mainDiv.style.boxShadow = "4px 4px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)"; mainDiv.style.display = 'flex'; mainDiv.style.flexDirection = 'column'; mainDiv.style.fontFamily = 'Tahoma, Geneva, sans-serif'; document.body.appendChild(mainDiv); // Header let headerDiv = document.createElement('div'); headerDiv.style.backgroundColor = '#000080'; headerDiv.style.color = '#FFFFFF'; headerDiv.style.padding = '4px'; headerDiv.style.display = 'flex'; headerDiv.style.justifyContent = 'space-between'; headerDiv.innerHTML = 'Final Review: Polls vs. Reality'; let closeBtn = document.createElement('button'); closeBtn.innerText = 'X'; closeBtn.style.fontWeight = 'bold'; closeBtn.style.marginLeft = '10px'; closeBtn.onclick = function() { mainDiv.remove(); }; headerDiv.appendChild(closeBtn); mainDiv.appendChild(headerDiv); // Content let contentDiv = document.createElement('div'); contentDiv.style.flexGrow = '1'; contentDiv.style.padding = '10px'; contentDiv.style.backgroundColor = '#FFFFFF'; contentDiv.style.margin = '5px'; contentDiv.style.border = '1px solid #808080'; contentDiv.style.overflow = 'hidden'; mainDiv.appendChild(contentDiv); const chartWrapper = document.createElement('div'); chartWrapper.id = 'poll_trend_wrapper_final'; // 使用不同ID防止冲突 chartWrapper.style.width = '100%'; chartWrapper.style.height = '100%'; chartWrapper.style.overflowX = 'auto'; const chartContainer = document.createElement('div'); chartContainer.id = 'poll_trend_chart_container'; // 必须匹配 render 函数里寻找的ID chartContainer.style.width = '100%'; chartContainer.style.height = '100%'; chartWrapper.appendChild(chartContainer); contentDiv.appendChild(chartWrapper); // *** 关键修改：传入 true，启用星星特效和 RESULT 标签 *** renderPollTrendChart(combinedData, true); } /** * 3. Check for Final Results Screen & Inject Button * 检测是否到达结局画面，并插入按钮 */ function checkForFinalScreen() { const footer = document.getElementById('map_footer'); const readingBtn = document.getElementById('recommended_reading_button'); // 条件：footer存在，reading按钮可见，且我们的按钮还没添加 if (footer && readingBtn && window.getComputedStyle(readingBtn).display !== 'none' && !document.getElementById('final_poll_chart_button')) { const myBtn = document.createElement('button'); myBtn.id = 'final_poll_chart_button'; myBtn.className = 'final_menu_button'; // 复用游戏原有样式类 myBtn.innerHTML = 'Poll Trend Chart'; // 样式微调，使其在最左侧 myBtn.style.marginRight = '10px'; // 绑定点击事件 myBtn.onclick = openFinalChartWindow; // 插入到 footer 的最前面 (最左边) footer.insertBefore(myBtn, footer.firstChild); console.log("Final Poll Chart Button injected."); } } // ================================================================= // VII. Updated Observer Logic (Override) // ================================================================= // 更新原有的 handleMutations 函数，或者创建一个新的 Observer 来运行 // 为了安全起见，我们添加一个新的独立 Observer 专门用于结局检测，以免破坏您上面的逻辑 const finalScreenObserver = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) { checkForFinalScreen(); }); // 开始监测 body finalScreenObserver.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true }); // 另外，为了防止现有 Observer 冲突，您可以在这里手动执行一次检查 checkForFinalScreen();
